There is nothing new under the sun. Don't get too lost in the ideas of individuality. Just follow your feelings, don't worry about what everyone says, even yourself.  You'll end up clipping the wings trying to not sound like the people who inspired you. Only writers worry about who's voice they hear when they write. True musicians can express themselves even using the same notes and rhythms of someone and something else. Originality doesn't matter as much as you think it does. The only thing that matters is sincerity. Everything else is dressing and trying to make money. That's another issue. You're inherently not expressing yourself, which is why the expressions of others resonate so loudly. But through these things you can better understand yourself. That is the whole reason to learn a song in the first place.  I couldn't write a good love song until i really connected and learned through an adele piece and felt her heartbreak. And then i saw a path to express my own.  After all Adele doesn't own the do wop changes, and i am no where near her skill level and i would be honored to be sued by the likes of her, but as the expression was my feeling, while i started in a someone like you feeling, i ended up in a mozarty sonata type of deal with the chords i like to use in my punk songs, especially hanging around the 4 and its dissonances in it's tensions to resolve that makes you want to depart immediately from the tonic to hang out in the dominant. It sounds triumphant in a minor key but devastating in a major key, at least with the tensions. But it can also be quiet, hopeful. The flexibility of expression that exists in something true, you almost dare the world to take you to court. Study the origins of melodies in popular music. Understand their meaning and the feelings. Then feel your own feelings and dare the world to tell you that you are not you. Mozart said he never cared about what anybody ever said, he only ever followed his feelings. Just don't be too German with that idea or you become a Nazi. But thats a history lesson, not a music one. But then again what do I know? I wrote my music for me, not for profit or for other people. And maybe the Door of the Sun will open. Shameless plug.

For anyone who wants to play the waltz  the chords: left hand plays: C2 and C3, then #G1 #G2, then F1 and F2 and G1 and G2 right hand plays: G3 C4 #D4, then #G3 C4 #D4, F3 #G3 C4  and  G3 #A3 D4  and the melody later on is C, C, C, C, B, C, D, bE, bE, bE, bE, F, G, bA, G, C, B, C  edit, the part after that melody is: C, C, C, C, C, B, C, D, F, G, G, bA, G, bE, C, G, bA, G, bA, G, bE, C  and btw the left hand malody keeps repeating  i only figured out the melody, thanks to the user "elric lescop" for the chords<3

Being a real songwriter, I can tell  you that it's really hard to come  up with something original today  because all the great melodies have  already been written.  Even if you  think you've come up with something new and exciting, a really  good musician will see that you've  either purposefully or accidentally stolen bits of a song that's already been written. I think it's hard to not write already existing songs nobody has ever thought about or at least get near to already existing songs. That's exactly why I stopped listening to popular music some time ago. It's always the same boring trash. That's also why dubsteb was interesting for a few years but the market got saturated soon. Everyone was able to do it on a PC without big prior knowledge and in a short time all songs became the same trash with too much fart sounds and base drops and sounded to close. And then everyone stopped listening to it. Music somehow needs a new innovation maybe someone can create a new cool instrument. So long I let time stand still and listen to music that was mostly made before I was even born.
